name:s‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äçy‚Äçs‚Äço‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçg
info:King Studio Suite
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Other
rating:5
posted:Posted February 10, 2024
msg:Challenge the Spring Festival in 2024 + Self-driving Tour + Electric Vehicle + Stay in Hotel/B&B with Cute Pets-Guiyang Station

This trip is the first time to stay in an international brand pet-friendly hotel. I only found this pet-friendly international brand hotel in Guiyang City. I bought a two-night package for 898 plus a single night stay for 497, with an average room rate of 465/night, including two breakfasts and unlimited coffee and tea. The hotel policy is to add an additional 200/time for dogs, which is quite reasonable. You need to sign a consent form before checking in. Except for the room and lobby, dogs are not allowed to enter the restaurant and other public areas.

üå≥Environment introduction:
The location in Guanshanhu District is a newly developed administrative district, not far from the museum, and it is also fast to drive to Jiaxiu Tower and Wenchang Pavilion. The hotel is close to the supporting commercial street of the community. If it is not the Spring Festival, it should be quite convenient, and it is also suitable for walking the dog.

üè†Layout/Room Type:
The room is about 40 square meters, with a small living room and a table with wheels. It is enough for two people and a dog. The bathroom is spacious and the toiletries are all in large bottles. It is also suitable for medium and long stays.

Our room faces the community with water views. Dog Baozi likes to stand in front of the floor-to-ceiling window to enjoy the scenery.

üíÅ Facilities and Services:
The 24-hour free self-service laundry room is equipped with different brands of laundry detergent and gadgets. There is a gym next to it, which is practical and comfortable.

The air conditioning temperature in the room is too high. It can reach 30 degrees even when it is turned off. You have to sleep with the window open in the winter.

[Bread] Breakfast:
Breakfast ends at 9:30. There is basically nothing to eat at 8:40. The restaurant is large and has enough seats. There are not many dishes. There is a noodle stall and an area for freshly fried eggs. The smiling service of the restaurant waiters and the timely prevention of smoking customers are deeply loved by me.

üèùTIPS for surrounding tours:
If you come to Guiyang for the first time, it is recommended to go to the Guizhou Museum first. For details, you can refer to the museum review I wrote [Leisure]

Finally, as a parent of a furry child, I am very happy to stay in this hotel. The service standards of an international brand, the geographical location, and the smiling service are the core values ‚Äã‚Äãthat I would recommend to my friends.
